The temperature was very high that day, nearly 30 degrees Celsius. When we entered the room, we turned down the air conditioner, but there was no cooling at all. After communicating with the front desk, the reply was that the air conditioner host had not been turned on. The reason was that the temperature in Duyun in March in previous years was not so high. The air conditioning system had not been cleaned and disinfected, so it could not be turned on for the time being, and only the air supply could be turned on. Later, the front desk suggested that we change the room to a different direction. Although there was no air conditioning, the windows in that direction were opened for natural ventilation, so it was relatively not so hot. The hotel is not small in scale, but it does not have its own restaurant (there is only a small restaurant that provides buffet breakfast), and you have to go out to find it yourself.
